The break statement in a block

  • - returns nil to method invoking the method yielding to the block when not passed an argument (FAILED - 1)
  • - returns a value to the method invoking the method yielding to the block

The break statement in a block yielded inside a while

  • - breaks out of the block

The break statement in a captured block when the invocation of the scope creating the block is still active

  • - raises a LocalJumpError when invoking the block from the scope creating the block (FAILED - 2)
  • - raises a LocalJumpError when invoking the block from a method (FAILED - 3)
  • - raises a LocalJumpError when yielding to the block (FAILED - 4)

The break statement in a captured block from a scope that has returned

  • - raises a LocalJumpError when calling the block from a method
  • - raises a LocalJumpError when yielding to the block

The break statement in a lambda when the invocation of the scope creating the lambda is still active

  • - returns nil when not passed an argument (FAILED - 5)
  • - returns a value to the scope creating and calling the lambda
  • - returns a value to the method scope below invoking the lambda (FAILED - 6)
  • - returns a value to a block scope invoking the lambda in a method below (FAILED - 7)
  • - raises a LocalJumpError when yielding to a lambda passed as a block argument (FAILED - 8)

The break statement in a lambda created at the toplevel

  • - returns a value when invoking from the toplevel
  • - returns a value when invoking from a method (FAILED - 9)
  • - returns a value when invoking from a block (FAILED - 10)

The break statement in a lambda from a scope that has returned

  • - returns a value to the method scope invoking the lambda (ERROR - 11)
  • - returns a value to the block scope invoking the lambda in a method (ERROR - 12)
  • - raises a LocalJumpError when yielding to a lambda passed as a block argument

Break inside a while loop

  • - stops a while loop when run
  • - causes a call with a block to return when run

Break inside a while loop with a value

  • - exits the loop and returns the value (FAILED - 13)
  • - passes the value returned by a method with omitted parenthesis and passed block (ERROR - 14)

Break inside a while loop with a splat

  • - exits the loop and makes the splat an Array
  • - treats nil as an empty array (FAILED - 15)
  • - preserves an array as is
  • - wraps a non-Array in an Array (FAILED - 16)

Executing break from within a block

  • - returns from the original invoking method even in case of chained calls (ERROR - 17)
  • - runs ensures when continuing upward (ERROR - 18)
  • - runs ensures when breaking from a loop
  • - doesn't run ensures in the destination method (ERROR - 19)
